  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_231e4423-8e3a-4a52-8c1b-e034b98d7605'
      });

<span id="freeTextContainer14267313752986926180">The Beast Within<br/>Blindfold, Inc., Book 1:<br/>Crystal and Daniel<br/><br/>Liz Cowan<br/><br/>A contemporary twist on Beauty and the Beast, with just a touch of magic to spice things up.<br/>Crystal Belle St. James’ life is demanding to the point of overwhelming.   <span id="freeText14267313752986926180" style="display:none">The Beast Within<br />Blindfold, Inc., Book 1:<br />Crystal and Daniel<br /><br />Liz Cowan<br /><br />A contemporary twist on Beauty and the Beast, with just a touch of magic to spice things up.<br />Crystal Belle St. James’ life is demanding to the point of overwhelming. Her days revolve around the thriving exotic plant and floral nursery. Her nights are devoted to caring for a parent suffering from Alzheimer's. She is lonely. But there are not enough hours in the day for a social life. <br />Reclusive Daniel Di Domenico may be handsome and wealthy but prefers solitude. No aimless thrashing about to find love for him. He doubts true love even exists.<br />Then Fate steps in. A brief glimpse of Crystal captures his interest. But before he can act on his desire to meet her, Daniel contracts Bell’s palsy and becomes temporarily disfigured. Just when he was ready to reach for something more than the status quo, his world becomes a cage of doctors and therapy. <br />Enter Blindfold, Inc. a unique dating service which allows couples to get to know each other without relying on a visual assessment of the other. On a Blindfold date, all the other senses come into play. They have the opportunity to discover the person behind the social mask. If they are lucky, they get to know their heart and soul.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2783945224" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12769779216564664440">This book is based around the beauty and the beast theme, a favourite of mine.<br/><br/>Daniel is a successful businessman, but his heart is guarded, not just for romantic love but relationships in general. When a medical condition changes his perspective, we get to see the real Daniel and his rather nice.<br/><br/>Crystal is the opposite of early Daniel in many ways, warm, caring and open. She also happens to run a successful business. <br/><br/>When I say caring, she really is, as she has been caring for her mother with ea</span>
  <span id="freeText12769779216564664440" style="display:none">This book is based around the beauty and the beast theme, a favourite of mine.<br /><br />Daniel is a successful businessman, but his heart is guarded, not just for romantic love but relationships in general. When a medical condition changes his perspective, we get to see the real Daniel and his rather nice.<br /><br />Crystal is the opposite of early Daniel in many ways, warm, caring and open. She also happens to run a successful business. <br /><br />When I say caring, she really is, as she has been caring for her mother with early onset dementia. I'm well aware of this disease and what it takes from the person suffering and their family and I felt the author covered it well. <br /><br />Daniel and Crystal together are sweet and sexy. They have a few issues to deal with in their story but generally it's easy reading.<br /><br />The magical part.... I wasn't sure of, I went with it but it was quite vague, think along the lines of 'the good witch' with extra seasoning.<br /><br />I really enjoyed the story and characters and I'm giving it 3.75/5 stars. The book could do with another quick edit, the odd name wrong and maybe taking a couple of Daniels love's out.<br /><br />I would recommend this book, I wanted to get back to it when I had to put it down. </span>
  <a data-text-id="12769779216564664440" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Our Book Club" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/67636305-our-book-club"><img alt="Our Book Club" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1494340330p2/67636305.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2366332221?book_show_action=true">Apr 19, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Our Book Club" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Our Book Club" href="/user/show/67636305-our-book-club">Our Book Club</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2366332221" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1229026399437578905">I have to say that I loved this book as I was reading through it because it was sooo smooth and sensual, romantic and blissful so yeah. It made me smile to myself as I visualized its two very much in love main characters Daniel Di Domenico and Crystal Belle St. James go about their relationship that unfolded over the course of the story. It is a charming tale and I absolutely loved its slow but enchanting flow because the author Liz Cowan’s style of writing is steady and smooth it does not bore </span>
  <span id="freeText1229026399437578905" style="display:none">I have to say that I loved this book as I was reading through it because it was sooo smooth and sensual, romantic and blissful so yeah. It made me smile to myself as I visualized its two very much in love main characters Daniel Di Domenico and Crystal Belle St. James go about their relationship that unfolded over the course of the story. It is a charming tale and I absolutely loved its slow but enchanting flow because the author Liz Cowan’s style of writing is steady and smooth it does not bore the reader (well for me that is) but seems to command one to complete it because Daniel and Crystal are so likable. They don’t have any traits that would cause me to dislike them. They are both decent adults with careers, with caring hearts for their parents and friends, I guess that’s why I love this book so much!<br /><br />For the curious, Daniel is the beast and Crystal is the beauty because well, Daniel woke up one morning to discover that he has Bell s palsy, and Crystal’s middle name is Belle so there’s that. All throughout the book, their relationship is one of love and loyalty. Before they met each other face to face, they dreamed about each other having pleasurable sex…and Daniel keeps on being mesmerized about the woman he saw at a gala for his great grandma which was Crystal. There is a little form of seriousness in this overly romantic and fairy-tale like story when Crystal becomes the source of one man’s obsession, a man other than Daniel who met Crystal one night when she went out with her two best friends. Other than that, the story is just pure consensual adult sex and good-natured sentiments.<br /><br />If I am going to recommend this book to someone, I would tell her or him to enjoy its likable, endearing main characters and to appreciate the light atmosphere it is set in. I also would tell them that the story is simple and not too complicated which would be enjoyed by those who prefer that reading level. I would remember to warn those who dislike romance and sexual content because Daniel and Crystal aren’t shy in that sense. Overall, I have to say that this was a breeze and should be read when you are not occupied with chores, errands, and other daily distractions. Honestly, I was in the midst of all those while tackling this beauty hence is why it took me 7 days to complete it. But I enjoyed it 100% so I believe you will too. Cheers!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1229026399437578905" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2526255199" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2526255199" />
    <a title="Shelby" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/80155104-shelby"><img alt="Shelby" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1523361799p2/80155104.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2526255199?book_show_action=true">Sep 11, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shelby" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shelby" href="/user/show/80155104-shelby">Shelby</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/80155104-shelby?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2526255199" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3385781889057128329">Overall rating: 1/5 I couldn’t finish this book. I love beauty and the beast stories but this just didn’t work for me. <br/><br/>DNF: 45% in<br/><br/>Heroine (Crystal): 2/5 She has a flower shop and takes care of her mother with Alzheimer's. She’s introverted and talks to herself a lot. <br/><br/>Hero (Daniel): 1/5 He is in the role of CEO of a finance company when he finds himself with a disease that messes with his face making him look like he had a stroke for a period of time. <br/><br/>Plot: 1/5 (I only made it halfway through the</span>
  <span id="freeText3385781889057128329" style="display:none">Overall rating: 1/5 I couldn’t finish this book. I love beauty and the beast stories but this just didn’t work for me. <br /><br />DNF: 45% in<br /><br />Heroine (Crystal): 2/5 She has a flower shop and takes care of her mother with Alzheimer's. She’s introverted and talks to herself a lot. <br /><br />Hero (Daniel): 1/5 He is in the role of CEO of a finance company when he finds himself with a disease that messes with his face making him look like he had a stroke for a period of time. <br /><br />Plot: 1/5 (I only made it halfway through the book) Daniel goes from being a hot, confident CEO to having the face of a stroke victim and is still a confident CEO. Crystal goes from being a flower shop owner taking care of her mom, to having her mom in an assisted living facility and is still a flower shop owner. Nothing other than meeting each other really changes about them, nothing about them needs to change. There was never any room for character growth as both are fine people from the get go. Which would be fine except for the plotline being based in the beauty and the beast fairy tale that is all about character growth. <br /><br />Personal Review: Daniel isn’t a bad guy, there is no lesson he needs to learn that would cause him to need this magical curse. He was hot before, and he had a heart of gold. Now he’s got a jacked up face and a heart of gold. For a beauty and the beast story to work the good looks of the lead need to be taken to give them a story arc; they are supposed to learn that beauty comes from within, etc. Here the guy was shown doing nice things for people from chapter one and denounces a pretty girl for being a mean character. There is nothing to be learned from the disfigurement.<br /><br />Everyone speaks like a predictive speech AI wrote the dialogue for the characters. Nothing they say comes across as genuine human interaction. Both leads constantly spew their stream of conscious out in dialogue mostly when they’re alone but they could be with other people as well, it was an odd writing choice to say the least. The story takes place in a contemporary setting and very much grounded in reality but has some magical elements that simply don’t jive with the setting. When a magical godmother is revealed she’s reacted to the same way I would react to seeing a friend with a nice haircut. This not a world where magic is widely known so I would have expected a bit more time in the freaking out stage than one line of dialogue. <br /><br />From the part of the book I actually read, I learned more about taking care of a parent with Alzheimer's than I did about this couple’s relationship. They don’t meet for real until 35% through the book but it’s a blind date (magic actually makes it so they can't see each other’s face like the episode White Christmas from Netflix’s Black Mirror). Reading about their date made me cringe rather than feel the warm and fuzzies. A big part of a beauty and the beast story is about Beauty accepting the Beast for his physical flaws because of his heart of gold. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3385781889057128329" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2590814384" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2590814384?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heather Strickland" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heather Strickland" href="/user/show/41708401-heather-strickland">Heather Strickland</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2590814384" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5808511049973516558">The Beast Within is the first book in the Blindfold Inc. Series by Liz Cowan. I received this book from NetGalley for an honest review. <br/><br/>This is a modern retelling of beauty and the beast. Daniel the beast in the in story prefers solitude to socializing. He seems to the outside world to be tough and uncaring. But he really does have a softer side. The reader sees this with Klaus Klieg bending his own rules. Daniel gives him money to keep Klaus's wife from getting his business in the divorce even </span>
  <span id="freeText5808511049973516558" style="display:none">The Beast Within is the first book in the Blindfold Inc. Series by Liz Cowan. I received this book from NetGalley for an honest review. <br /><br />This is a modern retelling of beauty and the beast. Daniel the beast in the in story prefers solitude to socializing. He seems to the outside world to be tough and uncaring. But he really does have a softer side. The reader sees this with Klaus Klieg bending his own rules. Daniel gives him money to keep Klaus's wife from getting his business in the divorce even though it is done in a stern way <br /><br />Daniel's parents had an arranged marriage. His mother, Layla left her husband Leonardo when Daniel turned 10. The plane she left on exploded. From the day his mother left and then died he made sure to never let any woman or anyone control his happiness. The only exception he was willing to make on love and trust were his paternal great-grandmother and Meredith. <br /><br />Meredith joined the family household when Daniel was born. She started as a nanny but her role grew to confidante and now Daniel's assistant. <br /><br />Crystal is the beauty in the story. Her mother at 40 was diagnosed with Alzheimer's. Her father, Colin was killed by a drunk driver. <br /><br />In contrast to Daniel's parents Crystal's had a very loving relationship. Crystal "yearned" for the type of relationship ship her parents had. But with so much on her plate those feelings and desires had to be put on hold. <br /><br />Roughly 25% into the book the story takes on a magical and fairytale aspect. Without giving anything else away this story does have a HEA. I cannot wait to read the next book in the Blindfold Inc Series. <br /><br />#TheBeastWithin #NetGalley #beautyandbeast #arc <br /><br /><br /> <br /></span>

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27349116-marsha-keeper-bookshelf?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27349116-marsha-keeper-bookshelf?shelf=keeper-bookshelf">keeper-bookshelf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27349116-marsha-keeper-bookshelf?shelf=z-keeper-bookshelf-2018">z-keeper-bookshelf-2018</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2538383632" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18125028578870544567"><a href='http://www.keeperbookshelf.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>Reviewed at Keeper Bookshelf</a><br/><br/>I love discovering stories with their own twists on the "tale as old as time" theme.  The Beast Within offers a unique take on the Beauty and the Beast idea with a couple who might have met under more usual circumstances if fate hadn't stepped in and changed everything.  Now they play out part of their romance through the anonymous dating of Blindfold, Inc. where each person meets without being face to face.  In many ways this allows a person's true self to show throu</span>
  <span id="freeText18125028578870544567" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.keeperbookshelf.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Reviewed at Keeper Bookshelf</a><br /><br />I love discovering stories with their own twists on the "tale as old as time" theme.  The Beast Within offers a unique take on the Beauty and the Beast idea with a couple who might have met under more usual circumstances if fate hadn't stepped in and changed everything.  Now they play out part of their romance through the anonymous dating of Blindfold, Inc. where each person meets without being face to face.  In many ways this allows a person's true self to show through, and in other ways it hides people until they are ready to be revealed.<br /><br />Crystal and Daniel's story is unique, realistic in the parts that others play in our lives and the hard fact that, to many, appearance does matter no matter how wonderful a person might actually be.  You'll find the cover description blurb does a very good job of setting up this romance.  There are harsh realities In Daniel and Crystal's story, each are dealt with gently yet realistically.  I was easily caught up in their lives both separate and eventually together.  If you enjoy not only Romance but variations on the Beauty and the Beast theme, then you'll enjoy The Beast Within.<br /><br />*I received an e-ARC of this novel from the publisher via NetGalley. That does not change what I think of this story. It is my choice to leave a review giving my personal opinion about this book.*</span>

<div id="review_2343271751" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2343271751" />
    <a title="Minion Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/80003590-minion-reviews"><img alt="Minion Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1522315959p2/80003590.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2343271751?book_show_action=true">Mar 29, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Minion Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Minion Reviews" href="/user/show/80003590-minion-reviews">Minion Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2343271751" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16813683754716562472">The Disney treatment of fairy tales has become increasingly popular in the last few years, thanks to live action remakes of Cinderella, Sleeping Beauty and, of course Beauty and the Beast. They have received huge commercial success, but I do find them a little old fashioned and naïve. I've grow out of the sugary sweetness of the Disney versions, but I do still enjoy the basis plot of these stories that go back hundreds of years. So I was delighted to find a modern treatment of Beauty and the Bea</span>
  <span id="freeText16813683754716562472" style="display:none">The Disney treatment of fairy tales has become increasingly popular in the last few years, thanks to live action remakes of Cinderella, Sleeping Beauty and, of course Beauty and the Beast. They have received huge commercial success, but I do find them a little old fashioned and naïve. I've grow out of the sugary sweetness of the Disney versions, but I do still enjoy the basis plot of these stories that go back hundreds of years. So I was delighted to find a modern treatment of Beauty and the Beast, with 'The Beast Within' by Liz Cowan. It follows the plot of a disfigured man falling for a beautiful woman, but with help of a unique dating service, instead of castle imprisonment.<br /><br />It may seem like this version of the classic Beauty and the beast story is not very magical, but it was still very enchanting and beautiful, thanks to Cowan's dreamy writing style. Furthermore, her characters are beautifully developed throughout the book, and are so empathetic you will become invested in their outcome. This was particularly true for Crystal Belle St. James, who represents so many of today's women, with a life so hectic and demanding that she is on the brink of losing herself.<br /><br />A lovely read, perfect for a rainy weekend. Highly recommended.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16813683754716562472" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="CGY Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/80007601-cgy-reviews"><img alt="CGY Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1522324658p2/80007601.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2343336700?book_show_action=true">Mar 29, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="CGY Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="CGY Reviews" href="/user/show/80007601-cgy-reviews">CGY Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2343336700" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7434926674274903158">Imagine a cross between Beauty and the beast, Fifty Shades of Grey, and Black Mirror, and you have The Beast Within, the first novel in the Blindfold Inc, series by Liz Cowan. It follows the story of cynical Daniel Di Domenico, who has no interest in love until he has a chance glimpse of florist Crystal Belle St. James. Ironically, just as he discovers love, he is stuck down with Bell's Palsy and suffers a crisis of confidence. Step in the mysterious dating agency, Blindfold Inc. who will facili</span>
  <span id="freeText7434926674274903158" style="display:none">Imagine a cross between Beauty and the beast, Fifty Shades of Grey, and Black Mirror, and you have The Beast Within, the first novel in the Blindfold Inc, series by Liz Cowan. It follows the story of cynical Daniel Di Domenico, who has no interest in love until he has a chance glimpse of florist Crystal Belle St. James. Ironically, just as he discovers love, he is stuck down with Bell's Palsy and suffers a crisis of confidence. Step in the mysterious dating agency, Blindfold Inc. who will facilitate couples getting to know each other, with the absence of one of their senses...sight. Will the two fall in love with the person within, is there really more to attraction that physical appearances.<br /><br />I really enjoyed Cowan's modern version of the love story, it definitely help my attention. Well-written, well-thought out and quite the page turner. Wonder what fairytale she will give her unique twist to next? Sleeping Beauty maybe, perhaps Cinderella? Who knows, all I know, is that I am looking forward to Book 2.<br /></span>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText12285290125356283435" style="display:none">“Daniel was well and truly captivated by the mystery woman in red...Whoever she was, she held Daniel spellbound...For a fraction of a second her sapphire eyes connected with his. <div id="review_2385541744" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2385541744" />
    <a title="Book Blast" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/72437516-book-blast"><img alt="Book Blast" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1519305008p2/72437516.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2385541744?book_show_action=true">May 08, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Book Blast" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Book Blast" href="/user/show/72437516-book-blast">Book Blast</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2385541744" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14403332218326603372">The Beast Within by Liz Cowan is a contemporary re-telling of the classic story Beauty and the Beast. With the modern touches, this story is transformed from an overly saccharine love story into one that is both realistic and touching. Crystal Belle St. James is the lead character with a simply overwhelming life. With a business to run, and familial obligations, she has little time for anything else, especially love or romance. However, things take a dramatic turn, and she meets Daniel. Daniel i</span>
  <span id="freeText14403332218326603372" style="display:none">The Beast Within by Liz Cowan is a contemporary re-telling of the classic story Beauty and the Beast. With the modern touches, this story is transformed from an overly saccharine love story into one that is both realistic and touching. Crystal Belle St. James is the lead character with a simply overwhelming life. With a business to run, and familial obligations, she has little time for anything else, especially love or romance. However, things take a dramatic turn, and she meets Daniel. Daniel is no ordinary man though, after being disfigured with Bell's palsy, his life changes radically. Through a specialized dating service called Blind Inc., they begin a relationship they never anticipated. This is a great book that will appeal to your softer side, rooting for the underdog, and hoping for the best outcome for all involved. The author writes with a beautiful touch, and even though the tone of the story may be somewhat sad, the characters carry the story with depth and emotion. Highly recommend for a sweet and involving story that is different from your basic romance.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14403332218326603372" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText3517261548607036373" style="display:none">The Beast Within by Liz Cowan is book One in the Blindfold, Inc series. This is the story of Crystal Belle St. James and Daniel Di Domenico. <br />Daniel's mother left him when he was around 10 years old..which broke his heart. Now all those years later he is all business and doens't really believe in love. But a chance siting of a women that somehow touched the loneliness he has been feeling. Crystal owns a flower shop which she loves and works hard to keep it going. But Crystal also has a mother who has Alzheimer which keeps her busy too. With no free time for a social life she is lonely. Crystal is at the point where she can do nothing else for her mother but put her in a secure nursing home. Before Daniel can go forward with following up with his brief glimpse of Crystal he gets Bell's palsy, which is a temporary but it makes him feel very self conscious. But fate has a way of connecting these two lonely hearts together. <br /> </span>

<div id="review_2387360123" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2387360123" />
    <a title="Page After Page" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/72617110-page-after-page"><img alt="Page After Page" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1517234316p2/72617110.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2387360123?book_show_action=true">May 10, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Page After Page" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Page After Page" href="/user/show/72617110-page-after-page">Page After Page</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2387360123" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10915976687292616958">2018 was the year I decided to branch out of my normal thriller or horror reads. It isn't that I don't love them, but sometimes you need a change, to stop one book from blending into another. So I thought why not give romance a try, but I didn't want the standard, soppy, over-the-top, style of love story, I wanted something a little bit more up-to-date. This led me to Liz Cowan and her book The Beast Within.<br/><br/>It seems fate has destined a couple to meet, but barriers come up thick and fast, attempt</span>
  <span id="freeText10915976687292616958" style="display:none">2018 was the year I decided to branch out of my normal thriller or horror reads. It isn't that I don't love them, but sometimes you need a change, to stop one book from blending into another. So I thought why not give romance a try, but I didn't want the standard, soppy, over-the-top, style of love story, I wanted something a little bit more up-to-date. This led me to Liz Cowan and her book The Beast Within.<br /><br />It seems fate has destined a couple to meet, but barriers come up thick and fast, attempting to keep them apart. I surprised myself my becoming increasingly invested in the romance between Crystal and Daniel, the main protagonists, that I had to keep reading, chapter after chapter. I stayed up way past my bedtime to finish, but the ending made it worth it. The writing style flows nicely, it is a little raunchy in parts, but I think it makes the romance and plot more realistic. Good work, Liz Cowan, I shall be eagerly awaiting the next romance helped by Blindfold Inc.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10915976687292616958" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2332074692" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2332074692" />
    <a title="MP" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/79564120-mp"><img alt="MP" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2332074692?book_show_action=true">Mar 18, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="MP" class="user" itemprop="url" name="MP" href="/user/show/79564120-mp">MP</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2332074692" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5610665554882586158">A modern twist on the old tale, "The Beast Within" surprised me with its humor and blending of genres. Something in the story that particularly touched me was the description of a family dealing with Alzheimer's disease. Their heartache over the disease was so well written that it really connected me with those characters. For readers who don't like curse words, I would caution you that this book utilizes those.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2556505977" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2556505977" />
    <a title="Wanda" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17164155-wanda"><img alt="Wanda" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1372433062p2/17164155.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2556505977?book_show_action=true">Oct 09, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wanda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wanda" href="/user/show/17164155-wanda">Wanda</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2556505977" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15340015446831407193">I was expecting a little bit more from this book, i was disappointed. It was a modern twist on the old tale, "The Beast Within". The story that was touching to me was the description of a family dealing with Alzheimer's disease. It seems to common now a day. The heartache over the disease was very well written by the author. Over all a good book.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_38343303'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/38343303-chasing-the-red-queen"><img alt="Chasing the Red Queen" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1517722141l/38343303._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('AvwtKRxNQtYd6bjckGO3J4jUFlb2A1aLCYJ3qwozh58dzBf8PGtIekAzUK+FLZ47dnKmjteA5BveHh480uJdTw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('N87ldS6cs/tvi0ZeEuwZ7HW86gU9PJam4nOhcm0OY24o/t+gDrq5VzJRri0HojDwixpa3Ry/JDY178jltd+5vg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
